*Offering LinkedIn Career Kickstarter Program | 12th December 2023 |*

Dear Students,

Greetings from Dr. D. Y. Patil Educational Complex, Akurdi, Pune !

The details of  #LinkedInCareerKickstarter program are shared as below:

LinkedIn in their career-building while at college. As a part of this #LinkedInCareerKickstarter program, we offer their LinkedIn Premium services to the students of our partner institutions completely free of cost. 

We have helped 5L+ students and 3K+ faculties through this program in the previous academic year 2022 - 2023. Based on the positive feedback from the students on how this program has helped them improve their career prospects and institutions requesting to extend this to the incoming batch, LinkedIn has accepted to extend the timeline of this project. 

LinkedIn Premium services offer a host of benefits to students, We see three major areas through which the students can directly realize the value
Learning: Students can learn from a bouquet of courses across domains in Technology, Skills & Certifications
Professional Networking: Students would be able to directly connect with recruiters/industry leaders for mentorship and guidance through InMail credit
Land Internships: LinkedIn has been a great platform to network and land jobs and internships
The session regarding the registration process is arranged as below

Date - 12th December 2023
Time - 12 noon.
Venue - Shantai Auditorium 

ALL STUDENTS SHOULD REGISTER IN THE LINK *ON OR BEFORE 09th DECEMBER 2023, 2PM.*

*Registration Link - https://forms.gle/Qz4rz3qQUP9ik5oj6*

*Corporate Relations & Placement Cell*
*Dr. D. Y. Patil Educational Complex, Akurdi, Pune*

15/09/2024, 11:24â€¯am - Onkar Shinde: Scanner sc = new Scanner(System.in);
		int T = sc.nextInt();
		while(T>0){
		    int l = sc.nextInt();
		    int arr[] = new int[l];
		    for(int i=0;i<l;i++){
                arr[i] = sc.nextInt();
		    }
		    HashMap<Integer,Integer> map = new HashMap();
		
		    for(int i=0;i<l;i++){
		        if(map.containsKey(arr[i])){
		            map.put(arr[i],map.get(arr[i])+1);
		        }else{
		            map.put(arr[i],1);
		        }
		    }
		    int max1=0,num1=0;
		    for(Integer key : map.keySet()){
		        if(max1<map.get(key)){
		            max1 = map.get(key);
		            num1 = key;
		        } 
		    }
		    map.remove(num1);
		    int max2=0,num2=0;
		    for(Integer key : map.keySet()){
		        if(max2<map.get(key)) {
		           max2 = map.get(key);
		           num2= key;
		       }
		    }
		    if(max1==max2){
		        System.out.println("CONFUSED");
		    }else{
		        System.out.println(num1);
		    }
		    T--;
		}

22/11/2024, 12:57â€¯am - Onkar Shinde: class Solution {
    public boolean path(Node root,int n1,ArrayList<Integer> list){
        if(root==null) return false;
        if(root.data==n1) return true;
        list.add(root.data);
        boolean left = path(root.left,n1,list);
        if(left){
            return true;
        }
        boolean right = path(root.right,n1,list);
        if(right){
            return true;
        }
        list.remove(list.size()-1);
        return false;
    }
    public ArrayList<Integer> Ancestors(Node root, int target) {
        ArrayList<Integer> list = new ArrayList();
        path(root,target,list);
        Collections.reverse(list);
        return list;
    }
}
